 a division bench of Justice BS Chauhan and Justice SA Bobde said that advocacy was once known as an elite profession but in the current era this profession has turned into a professional assurance
 mukadmaa ladanaa itnaa manhagaa ho gaya he ki ek garib aadmi kii pahunch se yah dur ho chukaa he
 The judges said that lawyers have equal involvement with the judges in the administration of justice and lawyers cannot conduct themselves like suspects or just living with the help of lawsuits
 nyaayalay ne kaha ki kisi vakil dwaara jaanboojh kar vaadakari ke hiton kii andekhi karnaa ek vakil ke anuroop nahin he

 ek vakil adaalat kaa adhikari he or is naate uskaa yah kartavya he ki vah sucharu dhang se nyaayalay kaa kaamkaaj sunishchat kare

 nyaayalay ne kaha ki kanoon vyapaar nahin he

 ) a Brazilian doctor is suspected of killing seven patients to evacuate the hospital
 dakshini brazil kii is ghatana ko lekar 300 anya marijon kii hatya kiye jane kii jaanch kii ja rahi he
 This information was given by the investigators
 samachar agency sinhua ke mutabik swasthya mantralay ke jaanchakarta mario lobato ke netritv main ek team pichley saat varshon ke dauraan dakshin parana praant ke shahar couritiba main evaingelico aspataal main varjeenia soars kii dekharekh vaale saghan chikitsa kaksh main hui 1,872 mauton kii jaanch kar rahi he
 According to public prosecutors, Soars and his medical team administered the drugs to the patients of the unit admitted to the muscles and lowered their oxygen supply which caused respiratory obstruction
 abhiyojkon ne kaha he ki is baat kaa khulaasa telephone tanping se hua jisamen unhone paaya ki soars ne ikai ke bistaron ko khaali karne ke liye marijon kii hatya kii he
 The 56-year-old widow was arrested in February along with three other physicians and three nurses and a physiotherapist
 sabhi ko saat hatyaon kaa aaropee banaaya gaya he
 The comments ravivaar ko lobato ne brazil ke globo tivi ko bataaya ki 20 mautein sandigdh lag rahi hai or anya 300 mauton kii jaanch kii ja rahi he
 Signs of muscle loss and oxygen deficiency have been found in all
 yadi abhiyojak sabit kar dete hai ki soars ne 300 rogiyon kii hatya kii he to yah duniya kaa sabase bhishantam shrinkhalabaddh hatya mana jayega
 Soars denied the allegations at the time of his arrest

 Earlier, she made a new history by entering the Olympic Games gymnastics event after 52 years as the first Indian female athlete

 Deepa, India's first female gymnast, will now compete for a medal in the final of the vault event on 14 February
 deepa ab final kii taiyaariyon main vyast hai
 His father and weightlifting coach at Sports Authority of India (sai) and his mother will perform a special puja on Tuesday
 deepa mangalvaar ko 23 saal kii ho jaaengi or unki jeet ke liye is khaas puja kaa aayojan kiya ja rahaa he
 Sai's coach and Deepa's father Dulal Karmakar told IANS, "not only are we all happy, but every Indian is celebrating the good news of Deepa reaching the final of the Olympics
 visheshkar tripura ke log
 " deepa kii maa gauri devi ne kaha, "hamaara itnaa purana sapana puraa ho gaya he, kyonki hamaari beti rio olympic ke final main pahunch gai he
 "during this time there were tears of joy in his eyes
 gauri devi ne kaha, "kal deepa kaa 23waan janmdin he
 Our daughter is away from home
 isliye, ham uske janmdin par or final main uski jeet ke liye ek vishesh puja kaa aayojan kar rahe hai

 We came to know on Monday morning that Deepa had reached the final
 " deepa ke final main pahunchane kii khabar somvaar subah hi puure tripura main pahunch gai thi
 Tripura Chief Minister Manik Sarkar is a sports enthusiast and told IANS, “it is a time to be proud and celebrate
 main deepa ko kisi bhi prakaar kaa suzav nahin duungaa, kyonki vah behatar pradarshan ke liye sakasham hai
 "the government said," Not only India, but the whole world saw their performance
 " Congratulating Deepa and her coach Bishweshwar Nandi, Tripura's Sports Minister Shahid Chaudhary said that Deepa's success in gymnastics has made the people of the state and the country proud
 tippaniyan Chaudhary told IANS, “we wish him good health and his success in the final on 14 August
 puure bharat ko unase padak jeetne kii ummid he
 " deepa ko pichley saal arjuna puraskaar se sammanit kiya gaya tha
 India participated in gymnastics in 1964, 52 years ago
 ab tak 11 purush jimnast olympic khelon main hissaa le chuke hai
 Deepa's father said that before the competition started, her daughter called and told her that she was feeling very nervous

 Deepa is now busy with the final preparations
 unke pita tathaa bhartiya khel praadhikaran (sai) main bharottolan ke coach or unki mata mangalvaar ko ek khaas puja karenge
 Deepa will turn 23 on Tuesday and this special puja is being organized to win her
 sai ke coach or deepa ke pita dulaal karmkaar ne ieenes ko bataaya, "olympic ke final main deepa ke pahunchane kii khushkhabari na keval ham sab khush hai, balki har bhartiya jashn manaa rahaa he
 Especially the people of Tripura
 " Deepa's mother Gauri Devi said, "our old dream is fulfilled, as our daughter has reached the final of Rio Olympics
" " is dauraan unki ankhon main khushi ke aansu the
 Gauri Devi said, "tomorrow is Deepa's 23rd birthday
 hamaari beti ghar se dur he

 " Dulal said, "my family, relatives and neighbors were sitting in front of the television all night Sunday

 This is not a revelation or a confession

 It's not something i take any pains to hide, I'm not ashamed of it or particularly troubled by it

 i go quiet and it's difficult to get out of bed
 Like it always does the world around me loses focus and i struggle to make sense of it
 Sometimes these bouts last an hour - sometimes they last days
 Today, I'm on day 4
 i say i live with depression rather than i struggle with it because for me (and i speak only for myself here) i don't see why it has to be a struggle
 i once read an idea by an American essayist called Richard Mitchell which stayed with me; it's now become how i try to approach the dips in my week or month
 The idea is this: To be sick, or to suffer, is inevitable
 But to become bitter and vindictive in sickness and suffering and to surrender to irrationality, supposing yourself the innocent and virtuous victim of the evils intentions of the world, is not inevitable
 The appropriate answer to the question - Why me? is the other question - Why not me? *** Why am i writing about this? Well, i spend a fair amount of time on social media during the course of my day and today i found myself looking for something to post because it's been a few days since I've posted anything
 i couldn't find anything so i figured I'd just talk about this - how I'm doing, instead of what I'm doing
 It's as simple as that, and we could all stand to do a little more of it
 P
 S
 That picture just seemed to work in this context

 aaie jaanate hai vikram lander ke kaam ke bare main
 
 
 On September 3, the first deorbit, ie Vikram Lander, will change the class in the opposite direction, on September 3 at 8 am
 45 se 9
 Between 45 o'clock, Vikram Lander will leave the chase of Chandrayaan-2 orbiter and go to the new class
 tab yah 109 kimi kii apoji or 120 kimi kii periji main chand kaa chakkar lagayegaa
 It is called deorbit in scientific language, that is, moving in the opposite direction to the direction in which it was going
 orbitor se alag hone ke baad vikram lander 2 kimi prati second kii gati se hi chand ke chaaron taraf orbitor ke vipareet disha main chakkar lagayegaa
 This has been done because the orbiter will revolve around the moon at a distance of 100 km
 lekin, chand ke dakshini dhruv par jane ke liye vikram lander ko apni disha badalani hogi
 Therefore, he will have to go round the moon in the opposite direction
 4 sitambar ko chand ke chaaron taraf vikram duusari baar badalegaa apni kakshaisero vaigyanik vikram lander ko 4 sitambar ko shaam 3 se 4 baje ke bich chand ke sabase najdiki kaksha main pahunchaayenge
 The Apogee of this class will be 36 km and Periji 110 km
 5 or 6 sitambar ko lagaataar hogi vikram lander ke sehat kii jaanch4 sitambar ko duusari baar chand kii kaksha badalane yani chand ke sabase najdiki kaksha main pahunchane ke baad 6 sitambar tak vikram lander ke sabhi sensors or pelods ke sehat kii jaanch hogi
 The health of the Pragyan Rover will also be investigated
 7 sitambar hoga sabase chunauteepurn, chand par utrega vikram lander1:30 se 1
 40 o'clock at night (intermittent night of 6 and 7 September) - Vikram Lander will start descending to the south pole of the moon from a height of 35 km
 tab isaki gati hogi 200 meter prati second
 This will be a very challenging task for ISRO scientists
 1:55 baje raat - vikram lander dakshini dhruv par maujuud do cretar mengines-si or simpelius-en ke bich maujuud maidan main utrega
 From a height of about 6 km, the lander will land on the lunar surface at a speed of 2 meters per second
 ye 15 minute behad tanaavpurn honge
 3
 55 baje raat - landing ke kareeb 2 ghante ke baad vikram lander kaa ramp khulegaa

 5

 isi solar panel ke jariye vah urja hasil karegaa
 5
 10 baje subah - pragyan rover chand kii sataha par chalanaa shuru karegaa

 is dauraan vah 500 meter kii duuri tay karegaa
 Orbiter: isro's mobile command center 100 km above the moon, the orbiter of Chandrayaan-2 will send the information received from the lander and rover to ISRO center, orbiting 100 km above the moon
 isamen 8 pelod hai
 Also, the command sent from ISRO to the lander and rover
 ise hindustan aironautics limited ne banaakar 2015 main hi isro ko saunp diya tha
 Vikram Lander: ISRO built indigenous Landerlander on Russia's refusal, named after ISRO founder and father of Indian space program Vikram Sarabhai
 isamen 4 pelod hai
 It will carry out scientific experiments for 15 days
 isaki shuruaati dizin isro ke spes aplicoshan centre ahmedabad ne banaaya tha

 pragyan roverh is robot ke kandhe par puraa mishan, 15 minute main milegaa data27 kilo ke is robot par hi puure mishan kii jimmdari he

 chand kii sataha par yah kareeb 400 meter kii duuri tay karegaa

 phir chand se praapt jaankaree ko vikram lander par bhejega

 phir orbitor use isro centre par bhejega
